/* DROP TABLE */
DROP TABLE pcos.Member CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.qna CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.Board CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.Cart CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.Brand CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.Category CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.Product CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.OrderDetail CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.p_Order CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.Grade CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.AvgGrade CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.FAQ CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;
DROP TABLE pcos.boardbtn CASCADE CONSTRAINTS;

COMMIT;

/* Member (회원) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Member (
	email VARCHAR2(50) PRIMARY KEY,
	name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
	ageYear NUMBER(4) NOT NULL,
	gender CHAR(1) NOT NULL,
	skinType VARCHAR2(9) NOT NULL,
	phone VARCHAR2(11),
	zipcode CHAR(5),
	address1 VARCHAR2(200),
	address2 VARCHAR2(200),
	regStat CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL
);

/* OneToOne (1:1 문의) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.qna (
	qnaNo CHAR(17) PRIMARY KEY,
	title VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	contents VARCHAR2(1000) NOT NULL,
	recontents VARCHAR2(1000),
	regDate DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	replStat CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'N' NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL
);

/* Board (코스 커뮤니티 게시판) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Board (
	boardNo CHAR(19) PRIMARY KEY,
	title VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	contents VARCHAR2(1000) NOT NULL,
	regDate DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	readCount NUMBER(5) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	likeCount NUMBER(5) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	dislikeCount NUMBER(5) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL
);


/* Cart (장바구니) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Cart (
	cartNo CHAR(18) PRIMARY KEY,
	amount NUMBER(3) DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	productCode CHAR(13) NOT NULL
);

/* Brand (브랜드) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Brand (
	brandCode CHAR(1) PRIMARY KEY,
	brandName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL
);

/* Category (카테고리) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Category (
	categoryCode CHAR(1) PRIMARY KEY,
	categoryName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL
);

/* Product (상품) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Product (
	productCode CHAR(13) PRIMARY KEY,
	productName VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	productDesc VARCHAR2(1500) NOT NULL,
	price NUMBER(6) DEFAULT 0 NOT NULL,
	capacity VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
	image VARCHAR2(300) NOT NULL,
	categoryCode CHAR(1) NOT NULL,
	brandCode CHAR(1) NOT NULL
);

/* Order (주문) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.p_Order (
	orderNo CHAR(19) PRIMARY KEY,
	name VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL,
	zipcode VARCHAR2(7) NOT NULL,
	address1 VARCHAR2(200) NOT NULL,
	address2 VARCHAR2(200) NOT NULL,
	phone VARCHAR2(11) NOT NULL,
	payment CHAR(4) DEFAULT 'CARD' NOT NULL,
	comments VARCHAR2(100),
	orderDate DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	orderStat CHAR(1) DEFAULT 'Y' NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL
);

/* OrderDetail (주문상세) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.OrderDetail (
	productCode CHAR(13) NOT NULL,
	orderNo CHAR(19) NOT NULL,
	amount NUMBER(3) NOT NULL,
	price NUMBER(6) NOT NULL
);

/* Grade (후기/평점) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.Grade (
	gradeNo CHAR(19) PRIMARY KEY,
	comments VARCHAR2(1000) NOT NULL,
	grade NUMBER(2,1) NOT NULL,
	regDate DATE DEFAULT SYSDATE NOT NULL,
	email VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL,
	productCode CHAR(13) NOT NULL
);

/* AvgGrade (평균 별점) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.AvgGrade (
	productCode CHAR(13) PRIMARY KEY,
	avgGrade NUMBER(2,1),
	totalCount NUMBER(5),
	type1Count NUMBER(5),
	type1Avg NUMBER(2,1),
	type2Count NUMBER(5),
	type2Avg NUMBER(2,1),
	type3Count NUMBER(5),
	type3Avg NUMBER(2,1)
);

/* FAQ (자주하는 질문 게시판) */
CREATE TABLE pcos.FAQ (
	faqNo CHAR(2) PRIMARY KEY,
	title VARCHAR2(100) NOT NULL,
	contents VARCHAR2(2000) NOT NULL
);

/* 좋아요,싫어요 버튼 */
CREATE TABLE pcos.BOARDBTN (
	idx NUMBER(4,0) PRIMARY KEY,
 
	email VARCHAR2(50),
 
	boardno CHAR(19),
 
	likebtn NUMBER(1,0) DEFAULT 0,
 
	dislikebtn NUMBER(1,0) DEFAULT 0
);

COMMIT;



/*---------------------------------------------------------*/

/* OneToOne (1:1 문의) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.qna
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Member_TO_qna
FOREIGN KEY (email) REFERENCES pcos.Member (email)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

/* Board (코스 커뮤니티 게시판) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.Board
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Member_TO_Board
FOREIGN KEY (email) REFERENCES pcos.Member (email)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

/* Product (상품) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.Product
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Category_TO_Product
FOREIGN KEY (categoryCode) REFERENCES pcos.Category (categoryCode);

ALTER TABLE pcos.Product
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Brand_TO_Product
FOREIGN KEY (brandCode) REFERENCES pcos.Brand (brandCode);

/* Cart (장바구니) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.Cart
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Member_TO_Cart
FOREIGN KEY (email) REFERENCES pcos.Member (email);

ALTER TABLE pcos.Cart
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Product_TO_Cart
FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES pcos.Product (productCode);

/* Order (주문) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.p_Order
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Member_TO_p_Order
FOREIGN KEY (email) REFERENCES pcos.Member (email)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

/* OrderDetail (주문상세) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.OrderDetail
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Product_TO_OrderDetail
FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES pcos.Product (productCode)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE pcos.OrderDetail
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Order_TO_OrderDetail
FOREIGN KEY (orderNo) REFERENCES pcos.p_Order (orderNo)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

/* Grade (후기/평점) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.Grade
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Member_TO_Grade
FOREIGN KEY (email) REFERENCES pcos.Member (email)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE pcos.Grade
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Product_TO_Grade
FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES pcos.Product (productCode)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

/* AvgGrade (평균 별점) */
ALTER TABLE pcos.AvgGrade
ADD CONSTRAINT FK_Product_TO_AvgGrade
FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES pcos.Product (productCode)
ON DELETE CASCADE;

COMMIT;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_DELETE
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_DELETE" 
(
    v_boardno        IN      Board.boardno%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    DELETE FROM board
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno;
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_INSERT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_INSERT" 
(
    v_boardno       IN      Board.boardno%TYPE,
    v_title       IN      Board.title%TYPE,
    v_contents       IN      Board.CONTENTS%TYPE,
    v_email       IN      Board.email%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO Board(boardno, title, contents, email)
    VALUES (v_boardno, v_title, v_contents, v_email);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_SELECT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_SELECT" 
(
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT boardno, title, regdate, readcount, likecount, dislikecount
    FROM board
    WHERE  email = v_email
    ORDER BY boardno desc;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_SELECT3
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_SELECT3" 
(
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT * 
    FROM
    (
    SELECT boardno, title, regdate, readcount, likecount, dislikecount, rank() OVER (ORDER BY boardno DESC) rank
    FROM board
    WHERE  email = v_email
    )
    WHERE rank <=3;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_SELECTALL1
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_SELECTALL1" 
(
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT *
    FROM board
    ORDER BY boardno desc;
END;
/

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_SELECTALL2" 
(
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS

    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT *
    FROM board
    ORDER BY readcount desc,boardno desc;

--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_UPDATECONTENTS
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_UPDATECONTENTS" 
(
    v_boardno            IN     Board.boardno%TYPE,
    v_title            IN     Board.title%TYPE,
    v_contents            IN     Board.contents%TYPE
)
AS
BEGIN
    UPDATE board
    SET title=v_title, contents=v_contents
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_UPDATEONE
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_UPDATEONE" 
(
    v_boardno            IN     Board.boardno%TYPE
)
AS
BEGIN
    UPDATE board
    SET readcount=readcount+1
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno;
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_UPDATEONEDIS
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_UPDATEONEDIS" 
(
    v_boardno            IN     Board.boardno%TYPE,
    v_email            IN     Board.boardno%TYPE
)
AS
BEGIN
    UPDATE boardbtn
    SET dislikebtn=1
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno AND email=v_email;
    COMMIT;
INSERT INTO boardbtn(idx, email, boardno, dislikebtn)
    SELECT LIKE_SEQ.NEXTVAL,v_email, v_boardno, 1 FROM DUAL 
    WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT email FROM BOARDBTN WHERE boardno=v_boardno AND email=v_email AND dislikebtn=1);
UPDATE board
    SET dislikecount=1
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno
    AND EXISTS(SELECT email FROM BOARDBTN WHERE boardno=v_boardno AND email=v_email AND dislikebtn=1);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_BOARD_UPDATEONELIKE
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_BOARD_UPDATEONELIKE" 
(
    v_boardno            IN     Board.boardno%TYPE,
    v_email            IN     Board.boardno%TYPE
)
AS
BEGIN
    UPDATE boardbtn
    SET likebtn=1
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno AND email=v_email;
    COMMIT;
INSERT INTO boardbtn(idx, email, boardno, likebtn)
    SELECT LIKE_SEQ.NEXTVAL,v_email, v_boardno, 1 FROM DUAL 
    WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT email FROM BOARDBTN WHERE boardno=v_boardno AND email=v_email AND likebtn=1);
UPDATE board
    SET likecount=1
    WHERE boardno=v_boardno
    AND EXISTS(SELECT email FROM BOARDBTN WHERE boardno=v_boardno AND email=v_email AND likebtn=1);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_CART_CARTSIZE_BYEMAIL
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_CART_CARTSIZE_BYEMAIL" 
(
    v_email     IN  Cart.email%TYPE
)
AS
    v_record    NUMBER;
BEGIN
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO v_record
    FROM Cart
    WHERE email = v_email;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_CART_DELETE_BYCARTNO
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_CART_DELETE_BYCARTNO" 
(
    v_email     IN      Cart.email%TYPE,
    v_cartNo    IN      Cart.cartNo%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    DELETE FROM Cart
    WHERE email = v_email
        AND cartNo = v_cartNo;
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_CART_INSERT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_CART_INSERT" 
(
    v_cartNo        IN      Cart.cartNo%TYPE,
    v_amount        IN      Cart.amount%TYPE,
    v_email         IN      Cart.email%TYPE,
    v_productCode   IN      Cart.productCode%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    UPDATE Cart SET amount=amount+v_amount
    WHERE productcode=v_productCode and email=v_email
    AND EXISTS(SELECT amount FROM Cart WHERE productcode=v_productCode and email=v_email);
    INSERT INTO Cart(cartno,amount, email, productcode) 
    SELECT v_cartNo,v_amount,v_email,v_productCode FROM DUAL 
    WHERE NOT EXISTS(SELECT productcode FROM Cart WHERE productcode=v_productCode and email=v_email);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_CART_SELECT_ALL
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_CART_SELECT_ALL" 
(
    v_email       IN      Cart.email%TYPE,
    v_record      OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT c.cartNo, c.email, p.productCode, p.productName, c.amount, p.price, p.image
    FROM Cart c, Member m, Product p
    WHERE c.email = m.email
        AND p.productCode IN (SELECT productCode
                            FROM Product
                            WHERE productCode = c.productCode)
        AND c.email = v_email;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_CART_SELECT_BYEMAIL
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_CART_SELECT_BYEMAIL" 
(
    v_email       IN      Cart.email%TYPE,
    v_record      OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT * FROM Cart
    WHERE email = v_email;
END;
/

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_INSERT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_INSERT" 
(
	v_gradeno	IN      Grade.gradeno%TYPE,
	 v_grade		IN      Grade.grade%TYPE,
	 v_comments	IN      Grade.comments%TYPE,
	 v_email		IN      Grade.email%TYPE,
	 v_productcode	IN      Grade.productcode%TYPE
)
is
begin
	insert into grade(gradeno, grade, comments, email, productcode)
	values(v_gradeno, v_grade, v_comments, v_email, v_productcode);	
	commit;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_INSERT1
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_INSERT1" 
(
	v_gradeno	IN      Grade.gradeno%TYPE,
	 v_grade		IN      Grade.grade%TYPE,
	 v_comments	IN      Grade.comments%TYPE,
	 v_email		IN      Grade.email%TYPE,
	 v_productcode	IN      Grade.productcode%TYPE
)
is
begin
	insert into grade(gradeno, grade, comments, email, productcode)
	values(v_gradeno, v_grade, v_comments, v_email, v_productcode);	
    UPDATE avggrade SET 
    avggrade=(avggrade*totalcount+v_grade)/(totalcount+1),
    totalcount=totalcount+1,
    type1count=type1count+1,
    type1avg=(type1avg*type1count+v_grade)/(type1count+1)
    WHERE productcode=v_productcode;
	commit;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_INSERT2
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_INSERT2" 
(
	v_gradeno	IN      Grade.gradeno%TYPE,
	 v_grade		IN      Grade.grade%TYPE,
	 v_comments	IN      Grade.comments%TYPE,
	 v_email		IN      Grade.email%TYPE,
	 v_productcode	IN      Grade.productcode%TYPE
)
is
begin
	insert into grade(gradeno, grade, comments, email, productcode)
	values(v_gradeno, v_grade, v_comments, v_email, v_productcode);	
    UPDATE avggrade SET 
    avggrade=(avggrade*totalcount+v_grade)/(totalcount+1),
    totalcount=totalcount+1,
    type2count=type2count+1,
    type2avg=(type2avg*type2count+v_grade)/(type2count+1)
    WHERE productcode=v_productcode;
	commit;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_INSERT3
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_INSERT3" 
(
	v_gradeno	IN      Grade.gradeno%TYPE,
	 v_grade		IN      Grade.grade%TYPE,
	 v_comments	IN      Grade.comments%TYPE,
	 v_email		IN      Grade.email%TYPE,
	 v_productcode	IN      Grade.productcode%TYPE
)
is
begin
	insert into grade(gradeno, grade, comments, email, productcode)
	values(v_gradeno, v_grade, v_comments, v_email, v_productcode);	
    UPDATE avggrade SET 
    avggrade=(avggrade*totalcount+v_grade)/(totalcount+1),
    totalcount=totalcount+1,
    type3count=type3count+1,
    type3avg=(type3avg*type3count+v_grade)/(type1count+1)
    WHERE productcode=v_productcode;
	commit;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_SELECT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_SELECT" 
(
    v_email         IN      grade.email%TYPE,
    v_record       OUT      SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT  g.regdate, g.comments, p.productname, g.grade FROM grade g, product p
    WHERE email=v_email
    AND g.productcode=p.productcode;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_SELECT3
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_SELECT3" 
(
    v_email         IN      grade.email%TYPE,
    v_record       OUT      SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT * 
    FROM
    (
     SELECT  g.regdate, g.comments, p.productname, g.grade, rank() OVER (ORDER BY g.regdate DESC) rank
     FROM grade g, product p
     WHERE  email = v_email
     AND g.productcode=p.productcode
    )
    WHERE rank <=3;
END;
/

--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_SELECT_GRADENO

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_GRADE_SELECT_GRADES
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_GRADE_SELECT_GRADES" 
(
    v_productcode   IN  Grade.productcode%TYPE,
    v_record        OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT  * FROM grade g natural join member m
    WHERE g.productcode=v_productcode
    ORDER BY gradeno desc;
END;
/

--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_MEMBER_INSERT

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_MEMBER_INSERT" 
(
    v_email       IN      Member.email%TYPE,
    v_name       IN      Member.name%TYPE,
    v_ageyear       IN      Member.ageyear%TYPE,
    v_gender       IN      Member.gender%TYPE,
    v_skintype       IN      Member.skintype%TYPE,
    v_phone       IN      Member.phone%TYPE,
    v_zipcode       IN      Member.zipcode%TYPE,
    v_address1       IN      Member.address1%TYPE,
    v_address2       IN      Member.address2%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO Member(email, name, ageyear, gender, skintype, phone, zipcode, address1, address2)
    VALUES (v_email, v_name, v_ageyear, v_gender, v_skintype, v_phone, v_zipcode, v_address1, v_address2);
    COMMIT;
END;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_MEMBER_UPDATE
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_MEMBER_UPDATE" 
(
    v_email       IN      Member.email%TYPE,
    v_name       IN      Member.name%TYPE,
    v_ageyear       IN      Member.ageyear%TYPE,
    v_gender       IN      Member.gender%TYPE,
    v_skintype       IN      Member.skintype%TYPE,
    v_phone       IN      Member.phone%TYPE,
    v_zipcode       IN      Member.zipcode%TYPE,
    v_address1       IN      Member.address1%TYPE,
    v_address2       IN      Member.address2%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    UPDATE Member
    SET name = v_name,
        ageyear = v_ageyear,
        gender = v_gender,
        skintype = v_skintype,
        phone = v_phone,
        zipcode = v_zipcode,
        address1 = v_address1,
        address2 = v_address2
    WHERE email = v_email;
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_MEMBER_UPDATE_DEFAULTADDR
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_MEMBER_UPDATE_DEFAULTADDR"

    v_zipcode    IN      Member.zipcode%TYPE,
    v_address1   IN      Member.address1%TYPE,
    v_address2   IN      Member.address2%TYPE,
    v_email      IN      Member.email%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    UPDATE Member
    SET zipcode = v_zipcode,
        address1 = v_address1,
        address2 = v_address2
    WHERE email = v_email;
    COMMIT;

--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_ORDER_SELECT_ORDERNO

(
    v_orderno       OUT      SYS_REFCURSOR

    OPEN v_orderno FOR

END;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_PRODUCT_ORDER
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_PRODUCT_ORDER" 
(
    v_orderNo       p_Order.orderNo%TYPE,
    v_name          p_Order.name%TYPE,
    v_zipcode       p_Order.zipcode%TYPE,
    v_address1      p_Order.address1%TYPE,
    v_address2      p_Order.address2%TYPE,
    v_phone         p_Order.phone%TYPE,
    v_comments      p_Order.comments%TYPE,
    v_email         p_Order.email%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO p_Order(orderNo, name, zipcode, address1, address2, phone, payment, comments, orderDate, orderStat, email)
    VALUES (v_orderNo, v_name, v_zipcode, v_address1, v_address2, v_phone, 'CARD', v_comments, SYSDATE, 'Y', v_email);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_PRODUCT_ORDER_DETAIL
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_PRODUCT_ORDER_DETAIL" 
(
    v_orderNo       p_Order.orderNo%TYPE,
    v_productCode   Product.productCode%TYPE,
    v_amount        OrderDetail.amount%TYPE,
    v_price         OrderDetail.price%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO OrderDetail(productCode, orderNo, amount, price)
    VALUES ((SELECT productCode FROM Product
                WHERE productCode = v_productCode),
            (SELECT orderNo FROM p_Order
                WHERE orderNo = v_orderNo),
            v_amount, v_price);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_PRODUCT_SELECT_ALL
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_PRODUCT_SELECT_ALL" 
(
    v_record    OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT b.brandName, p.productName, a.avgGrade, p.capacity, p.price, p.image
    FROM Product p, AvgGrade a, Brand b
    WHERE p.productCode = a.productCode
        AND p.brandCode = b.brandCode;
END;
/

    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT *
    FROM Product p, AvgGrade a
    WHERE  p.brandCode= v_brandCode
        AND p.productCode = a.productCode
    ORDER BY a.avgGrade desc,p.PRODUCTNAME;

  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_PRODUCT_SELECT_MCATEGORY1" 
(
    v_categoryCode       IN      Product.categoryCode%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN

    SELECT *
    FROM Product p, AvgGrade a
    WHERE  p.categoryCode= v_categoryCode
        AND p.productCode = a.productCode
        AND p.productCode like 'M%'
    ORDER BY a.AVGGRADE DESC,p.PRODUCTNAME;
END;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_PRODUCT_SELECT_SEARCH
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_PRODUCT_SELECT_SEARCH" 
(
    v_search    IN      CHAR,
    v_record    OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
SELECT b.brandName, p.productName, p.productCode, a.avgGrade, p.capacity, p.price, p.image
    FROM Product p, AvgGrade a, Brand b
    WHERE p.productCode = a.productCode
        AND p.brandCode = b.brandCode
        AND (p.productName like '%'||v_search||'%' OR b.brandName like '%'||v_search||'%');
        END;
/

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_P_ORDER_SELECT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_P_ORDER_SELECT" 
(
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT p.orderno, p.orderdate, p.orderstat, od.amount, od.price, p.productname
    FROM p_order p, orderdetail od, product p
    WHERE  email = v_email
    AND p.orderno=od.orderno
    AND od.productcode=p.productcode
    ORDER BY orderno desc;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_P_ORDER_SELECT3
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_P_ORDER_SELECT3" 
(
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT * 
    FROM
    (
    SELECT p.orderno, p.orderdate, p.orderstat, od.amount, od.price, p.productname, rank() OVER (ORDER BY p.orderno DESC) rank
    FROM p_order p, orderdetail od, product p
    WHERE  email = v_email
    AND p.orderno=od.orderno
    AND od.productcode=p.productcode
    )
    WHERE rank <=3;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_QNA_INSERT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_QNA_INSERT" 
(
    v_qnano       IN      Qna.qnano%TYPE,
    v_title       IN      Qna.title%TYPE,
    v_contents       IN      QNA.CONTENTS%TYPE,
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE
)
IS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO Qna(qnano, title, contents, email)
    VALUES (v_qnano, v_title, v_contents, v_email);
    COMMIT;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_QNA_SELECT
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_QNA_SELECT" 
(
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT *
    FROM qna
    WHERE  email = v_email
    ORDER BY qnano desc;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_QNA_SELECT3
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_QNA_SELECT3" 
(
    v_email       IN      Qna.email%TYPE,
    v_record            OUT     SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT * 
    FROM
    (
     SELECT qnano, regdate, title, replstat, rank() OVER (ORDER BY qnano DESC) rank
    FROM qna
    WHERE  email = v_email
    )
    WHERE rank <=3;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_QNA_SELECTONE
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_QNA_SELECTONE" 
(
    v_qnano         IN      Qna.qnano%TYPE,
    v_record       OUT      SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_record FOR
    SELECT  * FROM qna WHERE qnano=v_qnano;
END;
/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL forPROCEDURE SP_QNA_SELECT_QNANO
--------------------------------------------------------
  CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE "SP_QNA_SELECT_QNANO" 
(
    v_qnano       OUT      SYS_REFCURSOR
)
AS
BEGIN
    OPEN v_qnano FOR
    SELECT  NVL(MAX(qnano),'qna_00000000_0000') qnano FROM qna;
END;
/
